[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m [prompt] system
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m [response] To find the expected win, we need to consider the probabilities of each scenario and the corresponding winnings. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin A:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Bin A has 1 white ball and 4 black balls, so the probability of selecting a black ball is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Black from A}) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin A:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{White from A}) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 3. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin B given a black ball from bin A:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Bin B has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7, so the probability of selecting a ball from bin B is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Ball from B} \mid \text{Black from A}) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 4. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin W given a white ball from bin A:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Bin W has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500, so the probability of selecting a ball from bin W is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Ball from W} \mid \text{White from A}) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 5. **Expected win if a black ball is selected from bin A:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The expected win if a black ball is selected is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Win} \mid \text{Black from A}) = 1 \cdot P(\text{Ball from B} \mid \text{Black from A}) + 7 \cdot P(\text{Ball from W} \mid \text{Black from A}) = 1 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + 7 \cdot \frac{5}{6} = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{35}{6} = \frac{9}{12} + \frac{70}{12} = \frac{79}{12}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 6. **Expected win if a white ball is selected from bin A:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The expected win if a white ball is selected is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Win} \mid \text{White from A}) = 8 \cdot P(\text{Ball from B} \mid \text{White from A}) + 500 \cdot P(\text{Ball from W} \mid \text{White from A}) = 8 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + 500 \cdot \frac{5}{6} = 6 + \frac{2500}{6} = 6 + \frac{1250}{3} = \frac{18}{3} + \frac{1250}{3} = \frac{1268}{3}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 7. **Total expected win:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The total expected win is the weighted average of the expected wins from each scenario, weighted by their respective probabilities:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Win}) = P(\text{Black from A}) \cdot E(\text{Win} \mid \text{Black from A}) + P(\text{White from A}) \cdot E(\text{Win} \mid \text{White from A}) = \frac{4}{5} \cdot \frac{79}{12} + \frac{1}{5} \cdot \frac{1268}{3} = \frac{316}{60} + \frac{1268}{15} = \frac{316}{60} + \frac{4536}{60} = \frac{4852}{60} = \frac{2426}{30} = \frac{1213}{15}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Therefore, the expected win is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \boxed{\frac{1213}{15}}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities of each scenario and the corresponding winnings. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Bin \( A \) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 3. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) given a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Bin \( B \) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 4. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) given a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Bin \( W \) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 5. **Expected win calculation:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The expected win \( E \) is the sum of the products of the probabilities of each scenario and the corresponding winnings:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E = P(\text{Black from } A) \times P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) \times \text{Winnings from } B + P(\text{White from } A) \times P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) \times \text{Winnings from } W
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Substituting the values we have:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E = \left(\frac{4}{5}\right) \times \left(\frac{3}{4}\right) \times 1 + \left(\frac{1}{5}\right) \times \left(\frac{5}{6}\right) \times 7
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Simplifying each term:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E = \frac{4 \times 3}{5 \times 4} + \frac{1 \times 5}{5 \times 6} \times 7 = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{5}{30} \times 7 = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{35}{30} = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{7}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    To add these fractions, we need a common denominator. The least common multiple of 5 and 6 is 30:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E = \frac{3 \times 6}{5 \times 6} + \frac{7 \times 5}{6 \times 5} = \frac{18}{30} + \frac{35}{30} = \frac{53}{30}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Therefore, the expected win is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \boxed{\frac{53}{30}}

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Bin \( A \) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \( A \), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \( B \). Bin \( B \) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$1 from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\$1 \text{ from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$7 from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\$7 \text{ from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) = \frac{1}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a black ball is selected from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Winnings} \mid \text{Black from } A) = \$1 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + \$7 \cdot \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \$5
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    If a white ball is selected from bin \( A \), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \( W \). Bin \( W \) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$8 from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\$8 \text{ from } W \mid \text{White from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$500 from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\$500 \text{ from } W \mid \text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a white ball is selected from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Winnings} \mid \text{White from } A) = \$8 \cdot \frac{5}{6} + \$500 \cdot \frac{1}{6} = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = \$90
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 3. **Total expected win:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The total expected win is the weighted average of the expected wins from both scenarios, weighted by their respective probabilities:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Total Winnings}) = P(\text{Black from } A) \cdot E(\text{Winnings} \mid \text{Black from } A) + P(\text{White from } A) \cdot E(\text{Winnings} \mid \text{White from } A)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Substituting the values we calculated:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Total Winnings}) = \frac{4}{5} \cdot 5 + \frac{1}{5} \cdot 90 = 4 + 18 = \$22
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Therefore, the expected win is \(\boxed{22}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m [ground_truth] \$20

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities and the corresponding winnings for each possible outcome. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Bin \( A \) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls, so the probability of selecting a black ball is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \( A \), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \( B \). Bin \( B \) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7, so the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The expected value of the winnings in this case is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Winnings} \mid \text{Black from } A) = 3 \times 1 + 1 \times 7 = 3 + 7 = 10
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    If a white ball is selected from bin \( A \), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \( W \). Bin \( W \) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500, so the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The expected value of the winnings in this case is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Winnings} \mid \text{White from } A) = 5 \times 8 + 1 \times 500 = 40 + 500 = 540
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 3. **Total expected win:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    The total expected win is the weighted average of the expected winnings from both cases, using the probabilities of each case:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Total Winnings}) = P(\text{Black from } A) \times E(\text{Winnings} \mid \text{Black from } A) + P(\text{White from } A) \times E(\text{Winnings} \mid \text{White from } A)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    Substituting the values we found:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    E(\text{Total Winnings}) = \frac{4}{5} \times 10 + \frac{1}{5} \times 540 = \frac{40}{5} + \frac{540}{5} = \frac{580}{5} = 116
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Therefore, the expected win is \(\boxed{116}\).

[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to calculate the expected value of the amount won based on the probabilities of selecting each type of ball from bins \(A\) and \(B\), and the corresponding amounts on the balls.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m First, let's define the probabilities and the amounts:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m - Bin \(A\) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls, so the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\) is \(\frac{4}{5}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m - Bin \(B\) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7, so the probability of selecting a ball labeled \$1 from bin \(B\) is \(\frac{3}{4}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m - Bin \(W\) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500, so the probability of selecting a ball labeled \$8 from bin \(W\) is \(\frac{5}{6}\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m The expected value \(E\) of the win can be calculated as follows:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m E = \left(\frac{4}{5} \times \frac{3}{4} \times 1\right) + \left(\frac{4}{5} \times \frac{1}{4} \times 7\right) + \left(\frac{1}{5} \times \frac{5}{6} \times 8\right)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Now, let's compute each term separately:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 1. The first term is the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\) and then a ball labeled \$1 from bin \(B\):
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \frac{4}{5} \times \frac{3}{4} \times 1 = \frac{4 \times 3}{5 \times 4} = \frac{3}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 2. The second term is the probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\) and then a ball labeled \$7 from bin \(B\):
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \frac{4}{5} \times \frac{1}{4} \times 7 = \frac{4 \times 1 \times 7}{5 \times 4} = \frac{7}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 3. The third term is the probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\) and then a ball labeled \$8 from bin \(W\):
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \frac{1}{5} \times \frac{5}{6} \times 8 = \frac{1 \times 5 \times 8}{5 \times 6} = \frac{40}{30} = \frac{4}{3}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Adding these three terms together gives the expected value:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m E = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{7}{5} + \frac{4}{3}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m To add these fractions, we need a common denominator. The least common multiple of 5 and 3 is 15:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \frac{3}{5} = \frac{3 \times 3}{5 \times 3} = \frac{9}{15}, \quad \frac{7}{5} = \frac{7 \times 3}{5 \times 3} = \frac{21}{15}, \quad \frac{4}{3} = \frac{4 \times 5}{3 \times 5} = \frac{20}{15}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m E = \frac{9}{15} + \frac{21}{15} + \frac{20}{15} = \frac{9 + 21 + 20}{15} = \frac{50}{15} = \frac{10}{3}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Thus, the expected win is \(\boxed{\frac{10}{3}}\).

Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to calculate the expected value of the winnings based on the probabilities of selecting each type of ball from bins \(A\) and \(W\). Let's break down the problem step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m ### Step 1: Calculate the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Bin \(A\) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m ### Step 2: Calculate the probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m ### Step 3: Calculate the probability of selecting a ball from bin \(B\) given a black ball from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Bin \(B\) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. The probability of selecting a ball from bin \(B\) given a black ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m ### Step 4: Calculate the probability of selecting a ball from bin \(W\) given a white ball from bin \(A\)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Bin \(W\) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. The probability of selecting a ball from bin \(W\) given a white ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m ### Step 5: Calculate the expected value of the winnings
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m The expected value \(E\) of the winnings is the sum of the products of each outcome and its probability. We need to consider both scenarios: selecting a black ball from bin \(A\) and selecting a white ball from bin \(A\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m E = P(\text{Black from } A) \times P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) \times \text{Value of ball from } B + P(\text{White from } A) \times P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) \times \text{Value of ball from } W
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Substituting the values we calculated:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m E = \left(\frac{4}{5}\right) \times \left(\frac{3}{5}\right) \times 7 + \left(\frac{1}{5}\right) \times \left(\frac{5}{6}\right) \times 500
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m ### Step 6: Simplify the expression
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m First, calculate the probability of selecting a ball from bin \(B\) given a black ball from bin \(A\):
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \left(\frac{4}{5}\right) \times \left(\frac{3}{5}\right) = \frac{12}{25}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Next, calculate the probability of selecting a ball from bin \(W\) given a white ball from bin \(A\):
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \left(\frac{1}{5}\right) \times \left(\frac{5}{6}\right) = \frac{5}{30} = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Now, calculate the expected value:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m E = \left(\frac{12}{25}\right) \times 7 + \left(\frac{1}{6}\right) \times 500
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m E = \frac{84}{25} + \frac{500}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m To add these fractions, find a common denominator. The least common multiple of 25 and 6 is 150:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \frac{84}{25} = \frac{84 \times 6}{25 \times 6} = \frac{504}{150}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \frac{500}{6} = \frac{500 \times 25}{6 \times 25} = \frac{12500}{150}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m E = \frac{504}{150} + \frac{12500}{150} = \frac{13004}{150}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m Simplify the fraction:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=2215262)[0m
